          --monorail-metadata-toggled-bg: var(--monorail-metadata-closed-bg);
        }
        mr-issue-page[codeFont] {
          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: flex-start;
          z-index: 200;
        }

          flex-wrap: no-wrap;

        }

          flex-grow: 0;

        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>

        <p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





I was working on a "Kiosk Mode Breakout" type of assessment where the only available application to the user is a current Google Chrome installation, heavily restricted by Chrome Browser Policies (



<span class="line"><!---->I was working on a "Kiosk Mode Breakout" type of assessment where the only available application to the user is a current Google Chrome installation, heavily restricted by Chrome Browser Policies (<!----></span>





https://support.google.com/chrome/a/answer/187202



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://support.google.com/chrome/a/answer/187202"><!---->https://support.google.com/chrome/a/answer/187202<!----></a>





)



<span class="line"><!---->)<!----></span>





 when I found a way to bypass the "Allow invocation of file selection dialogs" policy with Chrome internals.



<span class="line"><!----> when I found a way to bypass the "Allow invocation of file selection dialogs" policy with Chrome internals.<!----></span>



<br>





At chrome://webrtc-internals the two checkboxes "Enable diagnostic audio recordings" and "Enable diagnostic packet and event recording" in the "Create Dump" subsection open a (unrestricted by filetype) file selection dialog even if the Chrome Browser Policy "AllowFileSelectionDialogs" is set.



<span class="line"><!---->At chrome://webrtc-internals the two checkboxes "Enable diagnostic audio recordings" and "Enable diagnostic packet and event recording" in the "Create Dump" subsection open a (unrestricted by filetype) file selection dialog even if the Chrome Browser Policy "AllowFileSelectionDialogs" is set.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





VERSION



<b class="line"><!---->VERSION<!----></b>



<br>





Chrome Version: 86.0.4240.75 (Official Build) (64-bit)



<span class="line"><!---->Chrome Version: 86.0.4240.75 (Official Build) (64-bit)<!----></span>



<br>





Operating System: Windows 10 64bit Version 2004 (OS Build 19041.546)



<span class="line"><!---->Operating System: Windows 10 64bit Version 2004 (OS Build 19041.546)<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





REPRODUCTION CASE



<b class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION CASE<!----></b>



<br>





 - Set "AllowFileSelectionDialogs" policy to "Disabled" through GPO



<span class="line"><!----> - Set "AllowFileSelectionDialogs" policy to "Disabled" through GPO<!----></span>



<br>





 - Navigate to chrome://webrtc-internals



<span class="line"><!----> - Navigate to chrome://webrtc-internals<!----></span>



<br>





 - Click on either of the two checkboxes in the "Create Dump" subsection



<span class="line"><!----> - Click on either of the two checkboxes in the "Create Dump" subsection<!----></span>



<br>





 - Outcome: a file selection dialog opens



<span class="line"><!----> - Outcome: a file selection dialog opens<!----></span>



<br>





 - Expected outcome: file dialog does not open and Chrome reports "Access to local files on your machine is disabled by your administrator"



<span class="line"><!----> - Expected outcome: file dialog does not open and Chrome reports "Access to local files on your machine is disabled by your administrator"<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





FOR CRASHES, PLEASE INCLUDE THE FOLLOWING ADDITIONAL INFORMATION



<b class="line"><!---->FOR CRASHES, PLEASE INCLUDE THE FOLLOWING ADDITIONAL INFORMATION<!----></b>



<br>





no crashes triggered



<span class="line"><!---->no crashes triggered<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





CREDIT INFORMATION



<b class="line"><!---->CREDIT INFORMATION<!----></b>



<br>





Externally reported security bugs may appear in Chrome release notes. If



<b class="line"><!---->Externally reported security bugs may appear in Chrome release notes. If<!----></b>



<br>





this bug is included, how would you like to be credited?



<b class="line"><!---->this bug is included, how would you like to be credited?<!----></b>

<span class="line"><!---->Reporter credit: vvmute (Benjamin Petermaier)<!----></span>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.
